Notebook[{
Cell[TextData[{
 "Summer work done by Dan Moore and Dmitri Skjorshammer (with thanks to Jacob \
Lewis). This ",
 StyleBox["Mathematica",
  FontSlant->"Italic"],
 " file is to be used in conjunction with the provided magma code. The first \
example calculates the Picard-Fuchs equation for a two-dimensional reflexive \
polytope. The second example calculates the PF of the Skew Octahedron and \
computes its symmetric square root. The final part calculates the PF of \
WP(1,1,4,6). If the user wants to use the code to compute PF of other \
polytopes, it is suggested that they use the Skew-Octahedron example for \
\"general\" polytopes and if that doesn't work, should try WP(1,1,4,6)."
}], "Text",
 CellChangeTimes->{{3.487089241093769*^9, 3.4870894381014137`*^9}, 
   3.487979374090582*^9, {3.4879825247218924`*^9, 3.487982575865559*^9}, {

Cell[TextData[StyleBox["# v is the dual of the diamond, which I' m too lazy \
to look for in the database.\ndual = \
lattice_polytope.ReflexivePolytopes(3)[197]\ndiamond = dual.polar()\n\n\
var('z0 z1 z2 z3 z4 z5 z6 z7 z8 z9 z10 z11 z12 z13 z14 z15 z16 z17 t')\n\n# \
Construct the anticanonical, semiample hypersurface for this polytope\nv = \
diamond.points().transpose()\np = dual.points().transpose()\nmonomials = []\n\
for i in p:\n    term = 1\n    var_num = 0\n    for j in v:\n        if \
min(j) != 0 or max(j) != 0:\n            term_pow = 1 + j.dot_product(i)\n    \
        term = term * (eval(\"z\" + str(var_num)) ** term_pow)\n            \
var_num += 1\n    \n    monomials.append(term)\n#get rid of the terms \
corresponding to the origin\nmonomials = [ x / gcd(monomials) for x in \
monomials ]\n\n# the last element is always the one that has every point, so \
it gets a coefficient of t. \n# the others get 1's.\nmonomials[-1] = t * \
monomials[-1]\ns = sum(monomials)\nprint s\t\t\t\t\t\t# This is incidentally \
how the expression for s at the top of the .nb was made.\n\n\n# Now we want \
to make the toric variety.  First we need the complete fan.\n# Take the \
FaceFan of the diamond, then subdivide for every non-origin lattice point.\nf \
= FaceFan(diamond)\nfor p in diamond.points().transpose():\n    if max(p) != \
0 or min(p) != 0:\n        f = f.subdivide(new_rays=[p])\n\ntv = \
ToricVariety(f)",
 FontFamily->"Courier"]], "Text",
